//id:0FFF    itemName:黄铜巧匠手链
if(strcmp(itemName, "黄铜巧匠手链") == 0){
    return 0x0FFF;
}
//id:1000    itemName:以太黄铜手链
if(strcmp(itemName, "以太黄铜手链") == 0){
    return 0x1000;
}
